# 订单上下文数据库设计

**版本：V1.0**
**最后更新：2026-04-16**

---

## 一、概述

本文档定义订单上下文的数据库设计，包括实体、字段、索引、外键关系等。

---

## 二、实体清单

| 序号 | 实体 | 表名 | 状态 |
|------|------|------|------|
| 1 | SalesOrder | SalesOrder | ✅ 已完成 |
| 2 | OrderItem | OrderItem | ✅ 已完成 |
| 3 | CustomerProfile | CustomerProfile | ✅ 已完成 |
| 4 | ProductionStandard | ProductionStandard | ✅ 已完成 |
| 5 | ProductRequirement | ProductRequirement | ✅ 已完成 |
| 6 | StandardGradeMapping | StandardGradeMapping | ✅ 已完成 |

---

## 三、SalesOrder（销售单）

### 3.1 表名
`SalesOrder`

### 3.2 字段定义

| 字段 | 类型 | 必填 | 默认值 | 说明 | 生成方式 |
|------|------|------|--------|------|----------|
| Id | int | ✅ | 自增 | 主键 | 🔄 数据库自动生成 |
| OrderNumber | nvarchar(50) | ✅ | - | 订单号，唯一索引 | 👤 用户输入 |
| SignDate | datetime | ✅ | - | 签订日期 | 👤 用户输入 |
| CustomerId | int | ✅ | - | 外键 → CustomerProfile.Id | 👤 用户选择 |
| Status | nvarchar(20) | ✅ | 'Pending' | 订单状态 | ⚙️ 系统自动管理 |
| RowVersion | timestamp | ✅ | - | 乐观并发控制 | 🔄 数据库自动生成 |
| CreatedTime | datetimeoffset | ✅ | GETUTCDATE() | 创建时间 | 📅 系统自动赋值 |
| CreatedBy | nvarchar(50) | ✅ | - | 创建人 | 📅 系统自动赋值 |
| UpdatedTime | datetimeoffset | ✅ | GETUTCDATE() | 更新时间 | 📅 系统自动赋值 |
| UpdatedBy | nvarchar(50) | ✅ | - | 更新人 | 📅 系统自动赋值 |
| IsDeleted | bit | ✅ | 0 | 软删除标记 | 🗑️ 系统自动赋值 |

### 3.3 索引

| 索引名 | 字段 | 类型 | 说明 |
|--------|------|------|------|
| PK_SalesOrder | Id | 聚集 | 主键 |
| UK_SalesOrder_OrderNumber | OrderNumber | 唯一 | 订单号唯一约束 |
| IX_SalesOrder_CustomerId | CustomerId | 非聚集 | 外键列 |
| IX_SalesOrder_SignDate | SignDate | 非聚集 | 日期查询 |
| IX_SalesOrder_Status | Status | 非聚集 | 状态筛选 |

### 3.4 业务规则

- 订单号全局唯一
- 状态流转：Pending → Confirmed → Processing → Completed/Cancelled

---

## 四、OrderItem（销售项次）

### 4.1 表名
`OrderItem`

### 4.2 字段定义

| 字段 | 类型 | 必填 | 默认值 | 说明 | 生成方式 |
|------|------|------|--------|------|----------|
| Id | int | ✅ | 自增 | 主键 | 🔄 数据库自动生成 |
| SalesOrderId | int | ✅ | - | 外键 → SalesOrder.Id | 👤 用户选择/关联 |
| Sequence | int | ✅ | - | 项次号（订单内唯一） | ⚙️ 系统自动生成 |
| WorkOrderId | int | ❌ | - | 外键 → WorkOrder.Id | 🔗 创建工单后回填 |
| DeliveryDate | datetime | ✅ | - | 交货日期 | 👤 用户输入 |
| DelayPenalty | bit | ✅ | 0 | 是否延期违约金 | 👤 用户选择 |
| SettlementMethod | nvarchar(20) | ✅ | - | 结算方式（枚举） | 👤 用户选择 |
| MaterialName | nvarchar(20) | ✅ | - | 物料名称（枚举） | 👤 用户选择 |
| ProductionStandardId | int | ✅ | - | 产品标准ID | 👤 用户选择 |
| DeliveryState | nvarchar(50) | ✅ | - | 交货状态（枚举） | 👤 用户选择 |
| StandardGrade | nvarchar(50) | ✅ | - | 标准牌号 | 👤 用户选择 |
| PlantGrade | nvarchar(50) | ✅ | - | 工厂牌号（冗余） | 🔗 系统自动填充 |
| Density | decimal(18,4) | ✅ | - | 密度（冗余） | 🔗 系统自动填充 |
| OuterDiameter | decimal(18,3) | ✅ | - | 外径 | 👤 用户输入 |
| WallThickness | decimal(18,3) | ✅ | - | 壁厚 | 👤 用户输入 |
| Specification | nvarchar(50) | ✅ | - | 规格（外径*壁厚，冗余） | ⚙️ 系统自动生成 |
| OuterDiameterNegative | decimal(18,3) | ✅ | 0 | 外径下偏差 | 👤 用户输入 |
| OuterDiameterPositive | decimal(18,3) | ✅ | 0 | 外径上偏差 | 👤 用户输入 |
| WallThicknessNegative | decimal(18,3) | ✅ | 0 | 壁厚下偏差 | 👤 用户输入 |
| WallThicknessPositive | decimal(18,3) | ✅ | 0 | 壁厚上偏差 | 👤 用户输入 |
| LengthStatus | nvarchar(20) | ✅ | - | 长度状态（枚举） | 👤 用户选择 |
| MinLength | decimal(18,2) | ❌ | 0 | 最小长度（mm） | 👤 用户输入 |
| MaxLength | decimal(18,2) | ❌ | 0 | 最大长度（mm） | 👤 用户输入 |
| Quantity | int | ❌ | 0 | 数量（支数） | 👤 用户输入 |
| Meters | decimal(18,2) | ❌ | 0 | 米数 | 👤 用户输入 |
| ContractWeight | decimal(18,3) | ✅ | 0 | 合同重量 | 👤 用户输入 |
| TheoreticalWeight | decimal(18,3) | ✅ | 0 | 理算重量 | 🧮 系统自动计算 |
| Remark | nvarchar(500) | ❌ | - | 备注 | 👤 用户输入 |
| CreatedTime | datetimeoffset | ✅ | GETUTCDATE() | 创建时间 | 📅 系统自动赋值 |
| CreatedBy | nvarchar(50) | ✅ | - | 创建人 | 📅 系统自动赋值 |
| UpdatedTime | datetimeoffset | ✅ | GETUTCDATE() | 更新时间 | 📅 系统自动赋值 |
| UpdatedBy | nvarchar(50) | ✅ | - | 更新人 | 📅 系统自动赋值 |
| IsDeleted | bit | ✅ | 0 | 软删除标记 | 🗑️ 系统自动赋值 |

### 4.3 索引

| 索引名 | 字段 | 类型 | 说明 |
|--------|------|------|------|
| PK_OrderItem | Id | 聚集 | 主键 |
| UK_OrderItem_Sequence | SalesOrderId, Sequence | 唯一 | 订单内项次唯一 |
| IX_OrderItem_SalesOrderId | SalesOrderId | 非聚集 | 外键列 |
| IX_OrderItem_WorkOrderId | WorkOrderId | 非聚集 | 外键列 |
| IX_OrderItem_ProductStandardId | ProductionStandardId | 非聚集 | 外键列 |
| IX_OrderItem_StandardGrade | StandardGrade | 非聚集 | 牌号查询 |

### 4.4 业务规则

- Sequence（项次号）在同一订单内自动递增，从 1 开始
- Specification 自动生成为 {OuterDiameter}*{WallThickness}
- 当 LengthStatus = Range 时，MinLength 和 MaxLength 必须大于 0
- PlantGrade 和 Density 根据 StandardGrade 从牌号对照表自动填充

## 九、主外键关系汇总

| 子表 | 外键字段 | 主表 | 主键字段 | 关系类型 | 说明 |
|------|----------|------|----------|----------|------|
| SalesOrder | CustomerId | CustomerProfile | Id | 多对一 | 一个客户可以有多个销售单 |
| OrderItem | SalesOrderId | SalesOrder | Id | 多对一 | 一个销售单可以有多个项次 |
| OrderItem | WorkOrderId | WorkOrder | Id | 多对一 | 一个项次最终生成一个工单（可为空） |
| OrderItem | ProductionStandardId | ProductionStandard | Id | 多对一 | 一个项次引用一个产品标准 |
| OrderItem | StandardGrade | StandardGradeMapping | StandardGrade | 多对一 | 通过标准牌号关联牌号对照表 |
| ProductRequirement | OrderItemId | OrderItem | Id | 一对一 | 一个项次只有一个产品要求 |
| ProductRequirement | StandardId | ProductionStandard | Id | 多对一 | 多个产品要求可引用同一个产品标准 |

---

## 十、生成方式图例

| 图标 | 含义 |
|------|------|
| 🔄 | 数据库自动生成（数据库自增或默认值，无需代码干预） |
| 👤 | 用户输入（用户在表单中手动填写） |
| 👤 | 用户选择（用户从下拉框/单选/多选中选择） |
| ⚙️ | 系统自动生成（根据业务规则自动计算，如项次号、规格） |
| 🔗 | 系统自动填充（根据关联数据自动填充，如 PlantGrade、Density） |
| 🧮 | 系统自动计算（根据公式自动计算，如理算重量） |
| 📅 | 系统自动赋值（审计字段：时间、当前用户） |
| 🗑️ | 系统自动赋值（软删除标记，删除时设为1） |

---

======================================================================
FILE: docs\提示词.md
======================================================================

你是一位精通 .NET 8、EF Core 和 ASP.NET Core Web API 的高级后端开发工程师。

## 一、任务目标
为 MES 系统的“订单上下文”开发辅助实体的 Service 层和 Controller 层代码。

**涉及的实体：**
1. 客户档案（CustomerProfile）
2. 产品标准（ProductionStandard）
3. 牌号对照（StandardGradeMapping）

**注意：** 订单主表（SalesOrder）的 Service 和 Controller 已存在，不要重复生成。

---

## 二、现有文件（不要重新生成）

| 文件 | 路径 | 状态 |
|------|------|------|
| CustomerProfileDto.cs | MES.Core/DTOs/ | ✅ 已存在 |
| SalesOrderController.cs | MES.Api/Controllers/ | ✅ 已存在（代码风格参考） |
| OrderService.cs | MES.Services/Order/ | ✅ 已存在（代码风格参考） |
| 所有实体类 | MES.Data/Entities/ | ✅ 已存在 |

---

## 三、开发规范（必须遵守）

### 3.1 命名空间
| 类型 | 命名空间 |
|------|----------|
| DTO | `MES.Core.DTOs` |
| Service 接口 | `MES.Core.Interfaces` |
| Service 实现 | `MES.Services` |
| Controller | `MES.Api.Controllers` |

### 3.2 代码规范
- 使用 `async/await` 异步模式
- 使用 `BusinessException` 抛出业务异常
- Controller 返回 `ApiResponse<T>` 格式
- 所有公开类、方法必须有 XML 注释（`/// <summary>`）
- 花括号采用 Allman 风格（左括号换行）
- 依赖注入使用构造函数注入

### 3.3 权限规范
| 操作 | 角色 |
|------|------|
| 查询（GET） | `OrderStaff, OrderDirector, Admin` |
| 创建/更新（POST/PUT） | `OrderDirector, Admin` |
| 删除（DELETE） | `Admin` |

### 3.4 分页规范
- 使用现有的 `QueryParams` 和 `PagedResult<T>` 类

---

## 四、类型定义（重要！）

### 4.1 实体字段确认

**StandardGradeMapping 实体字段：**
```csharp
public class StandardGradeMapping : BaseEntity
{
    public string StandardGrade { get; set; }      // 标准牌号
    public string PlantGrade { get; set; }         // 工厂牌号
    public decimal Density { get; set; }           // 密度
    public string? HeatTreatment { get; set; }     // 热处理工艺
    public bool SpecialMaterial { get; set; }      // 是否特殊材料（布尔类型！）
    public string? SpecialNote { get; set; }       // 特殊注意事项
    public string? Remark { get; set; }            // 备注
}
```

**ProductionStandard 实体字段：**
```csharp
public class ProductionStandard : BaseEntity
{
    public string StandardCode { get; set; }       // 标准编码
    public string StandardName { get; set; }       // 标准名称
    public string? Remark { get; set; }            // 备注
    public int SortOrder { get; set; }             // 排序序号
    public bool IsActive { get; set; }             // 是否启用
}
```

**CustomerProfile 实体字段：**
```csharp
public class CustomerProfile : BaseEntity
{
    public string CustomerCode { get; set; }       // 客户编码
    public string Salesman { get; set; }           // 业务员
    public string CustomerUnit { get; set; }       // 客户单位
    public string? EndCustomer { get; set; }       // 最终用户
    public string? ContactPerson { get; set; }     // 联系人
    public string? ContactPhone { get; set; }      // 联系电话
    public string? Address { get; set; }           // 联系地址
    public CustomerStatus Status { get; set; }     // 客户状态（枚举）
    public string? Remark { get; set; }            // 备注
}
```

### 4.2 关键类型约束
| 字段 | 类型 | 说明 |
|------|------|------|
| `SpecialMaterial` | **bool** | 禁止转换为 "是"/"否" 字符串 |
| `Status` | `CustomerStatus` 枚举 | 使用枚举，不是字符串 |
| `SortOrder` | int | 默认值 0 |
| `IsActive` | bool | 默认值 true |

---

## 五、禁止事项

- ❌ 不要生成实体类（已存在）
- ❌ 不要生成 `CustomerProfileDto`（已存在）
- ❌ 不要在 Service 中将 `bool` 转换为 `"是"/"否"` 字符串
- ❌ 不要使用 `SpecialMaterial` 作为字符串类型
- ❌ 不要引入新的 NuGet 包

## 七、API 端点定义

### 7.1 产品标准 API

| 方法 | 路由 | 说明 |
|------|------|------|
| GET | `/api/standard/list` | 获取所有产品标准（用于下拉框，只返回 IsActive=true） |
| GET | `/api/standard/{id}` | 获取详情 |
| POST | `/api/standard` | 创建 |
| PUT | `/api/standard/{id}` | 更新 |
| DELETE | `/api/standard/{id}` | 删除 |

### 7.2 牌号对照 API

| 方法 | 路由 | 说明 |
|------|------|------|
| GET | `/api/grade-mapping/list` | 获取所有牌号对照（用于下拉框） |
| GET | `/api/grade-mapping/{id}` | 获取详情 |
| POST | `/api/grade-mapping` | 创建 |
| PUT | `/api/grade-mapping/{id}` | 更新 |
| DELETE | `/api/grade-mapping/{id}` | 删除 |

### 7.3 客户档案 API

| 方法 | 路由 | 说明 |
|------|------|------|
| GET | `/api/customer/list` | 分页查询客户列表 |
| GET | `/api/customer/{id}` | 获取详情 |
| POST | `/api/customer` | 创建 |
| PUT | `/api/customer/{id}` | 更新 |
| DELETE | `/api/customer/{id}` | 删除（仅 Admin） |

## 八、代码示例参考

### DTO 示例（ProductionStandardDto.cs）

```csharp
namespace MES.Core.DTOs;

/// <summary>
/// 产品标准 DTO
/// </summary>
public class ProductionStandardDto
{
    /// <summary>
    /// 主键
    /// </summary>
    public int Id { get; set; }

    /// <summary>
    /// 标准编码
    /// </summary>
    public string StandardCode { get; set; } = string.Empty;

    /// <summary>
    /// 标准名称
    /// </summary>
    public string StandardName { get; set; } = string.Empty;

    /// <summary>
    /// 备注
    /// </summary>
    public string? Remark { get; set; }

    /// <summary>
    /// 排序序号
    /// </summary>
    public int SortOrder { get; set; }

    /// <summary>
    /// 是否启用
    /// </summary>
    public bool IsActive { get; set; }
}
```

### Controller 示例

```csharp
[ApiController]
[Route("api/[controller]")]
[Authorize]
public class ProductionStandardController : ControllerBase
{
    private readonly IProductionStandardService _service;

    public ProductionStandardController(IProductionStandardService service)
    {
        _service = service;
    }

    [HttpGet("list")]
    [Authorize(Roles = "OrderStaff,OrderDirector,Admin")]
    public async Task<ActionResult<ApiResponse<List<ProductionStandardDto>>>> GetList()
    {
        var result = await _service.GetAllAsync();
        return Ok(ApiResponse<List<ProductionStandardDto>>.Ok(result));
    }
}
```

## 九、输出要求

1. **每生成一个文件后暂停**，等待我回复"继续"
2. **每个文件标注完整路径**，格式：`// 文件路径: MES.Core/DTOs/ProductionStandardDto.cs`
3. **每个文件输出完成后**，输出：`✅ 已完成 [文件名]，请回复"继续"生成下一个文件`
4. **所有文件生成完成后**，输出：`🎉 所有文件生成完毕`

FILE: MES.Api\Controllers\AuthController.cs

using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc;
using MES.Auth.Services;
using MES.Core.Models;
using MES.Core.DTOs.Auth;

namespace MES.Api.Controllers;

[ApiController]
[Route("api/[controller]")]
public class AuthController : ControllerBase
{
    private readonly IAuthService _authService;

    public AuthController(IAuthService authService)
    {
        _authService = authService;
    }

    [HttpPost("login")]
    public async Task<ApiResponse<LoginResponse>> Login([FromBody] LoginRequest request)
    {
        return await _authService.LoginAsync(request);
    }

    [HttpPost("logout")]
    public async Task<ApiResponse<object>> Logout()
    {
        return await _authService.LogoutAsync();
    }

    [HttpPost("refresh-token")]
    public async Task<ApiResponse<LoginResponse>> RefreshToken([FromBody] RefreshTokenRequest request)
    {
        return await _authService.RefreshTokenAsync(request.RefreshToken);
    }

    [HttpGet("current-user")]
    public async Task<ApiResponse<UserInfoResponse>> GetCurrentUser()
    {
        return await _authService.GetCurrentUserAsync();
    }
}

/// <summary>
/// 刷新令牌请求
/// </summary>
public class RefreshTokenRequest
{
    public string RefreshToken { get; set; } = string.Empty;
}

FILE: MES.Api\Controllers\CustomerController.cs

// 文件路径: MES.Api/Controllers/CustomerController.cs
using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Authorization;
using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc;
using MES.Core.DTOs;
using MES.Core.Interfaces;
using MES.Core.Models;

namespace MES.Api.Controllers;

/// <summary>
/// 客户档案控制器
/// </summary>
[ApiController]
[Route("api/[controller]")]
[Authorize]
public class CustomerController : ControllerBase
{
    private readonly ICustomerService _customerService;

    public CustomerController(ICustomerService customerService)
    {
        _customerService = customerService;
    }

    /// <summary>
    /// 分页查询客户列表
    /// </summary>
    [HttpGet("list")]
    [Authorize(Roles = "OrderStaff,OrderDirector,Admin")]
    public async Task<ActionResult<ApiResponse<PagedResult<CustomerProfileDto>>>> GetPaged([FromQuery] QueryParams query)
    {
        var result = await _customerService.GetPagedAsync(query);
        return Ok(ApiResponse<PagedResult<CustomerProfileDto>>.Ok(result, "查询成功"));
    }

    /// <summary>
    /// 根据ID获取客户详情
    /// </summary>
    [HttpGet("{id}")]
    [Authorize(Roles = "OrderStaff,OrderDirector,Admin")]
    public async Task<ActionResult<ApiResponse<CustomerProfileDto>>> GetById(int id)
    {
        var result = await _customerService.GetByIdAsync(id);
        return Ok(ApiResponse<CustomerProfileDto>.Ok(result, "查询成功"));
    }

    /// <summary>
    /// 创建客户
    /// </summary>
    [HttpPost]
    [Authorize(Roles = "OrderDirector,Admin")]
    public async Task<ActionResult<ApiResponse<CustomerProfileDto>>> Create([FromBody] CreateCustomerRequest request)
    {
        if (!ModelState.IsValid)
        {
            return BadRequest(ApiResponse<CustomerProfileDto>.Fail("请求参数无效"));
        }

        var result = await _customerService.CreateAsync(request);
        return Ok(ApiResponse<CustomerProfileDto>.Ok(result, "创建成功"));
    }

    /// <summary>
    /// 更新客户
    /// </summary>
    [HttpPut("{id}")]
    [Authorize(Roles = "OrderDirector,Admin")]
    public async Task<ActionResult<ApiResponse<CustomerProfileDto>>> Update(int id, [FromBody] UpdateCustomerRequest request)
    {
        var result = await _customerService.UpdateAsync(id, request);
        return Ok(ApiResponse<CustomerProfileDto>.Ok(result, "更新成功"));
    }

    /// <summary>
    /// 删除客户
    /// </summary>
    [HttpDelete("{id}")]
    [Authorize(Roles = "Admin")]
    public async Task<ActionResult<ApiResponse<object>>> Delete(int id)
    {
        await _customerService.DeleteAsync(id);
        return Ok(ApiResponse.Ok("删除成功"));
    }
}

using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Authorization;
using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc;
using MES.Core.DTOs;
using MES.Core.Interfaces;
using MES.Core.Models;

namespace MES.Api.Controllers;

/// <summary>
/// 牌号对照控制器
/// </summary>
[ApiController]
[Route("api/[controller]")]
[Authorize]
public class GradeMappingController : ControllerBase
{
    private readonly IGradeMappingService _service;

    public GradeMappingController(IGradeMappingService service)
    {
        _service = service;
    }

    /// <summary>
    /// 获取所有牌号对照（用于下拉框）
    /// </summary>
    [HttpGet("list")]
    [Authorize(Roles = "OrderStaff,OrderDirector,Admin")]
    public async Task<ActionResult<ApiResponse<List<StandardGradeMappingDto>>>> GetList()
    {
        var result = await _service.GetAllAsync();
        return Ok(ApiResponse<List<StandardGradeMappingDto>>.Ok(result, "查询成功"));
    }

    /// <summary>
    /// 根据ID获取牌号对照详情
    /// </summary>
    [HttpGet("{id}")]
    [Authorize(Roles = "OrderStaff,OrderDirector,Admin")]
    public async Task<ActionResult<ApiResponse<StandardGradeMappingDto>>> GetById(int id)
    {
        var result = await _service.GetByIdAsync(id);
        return Ok(ApiResponse<StandardGradeMappingDto>.Ok(result, "查询成功"));
    }

    /// <summary>
    /// 创建牌号对照
    /// </summary>
    [HttpPost]
    [Authorize(Roles = "OrderDirector,Admin")]
    public async Task<ActionResult<ApiResponse<StandardGradeMappingDto>>> Create([FromBody] CreateGradeMappingRequest request)
    {
        if (!ModelState.IsValid)
        {
            return BadRequest(ApiResponse<StandardGradeMappingDto>.Fail("请求参数无效"));
        }

        var result = await _service.CreateAsync(request);
        return Ok(ApiResponse<StandardGradeMappingDto>.Ok(result, "创建成功"));
    }

    /// <summary>
    /// 更新牌号对照
    /// </summary>
    [HttpPut("{id}")]
    [Authorize(Roles = "OrderDirector,Admin")]
    public async Task<ActionResult<ApiResponse<StandardGradeMappingDto>>> Update(int id, [FromBody] UpdateGradeMappingRequest request)
    {
        var result = await _service.UpdateAsync(id, request);
        return Ok(ApiResponse<StandardGradeMappingDto>.Ok(result, "更新成功"));
    }

    /// <summary>
    /// 删除牌号对照
    /// </summary>
    [HttpDelete("{id}")]
    [Authorize(Roles = "Admin")]
    public async Task<ActionResult<ApiResponse<object>>> Delete(int id)
    {
        await _service.DeleteAsync(id);
        return Ok(ApiResponse.Ok("删除成功"));
    }
}

using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc;

using MES.Core.Interfaces;

namespace MES.Api.Controllers;

/// <summary>
/// 订单控制器
/// </summary>
[ApiController]
[Route("api/[controller]")]
[Authorize]
public class OrderController : ControllerBase
{
    private readonly IOrderService _orderService;

    public OrderController(IOrderService orderService)
    {
        _orderService = orderService;
    }

    /// <summary>
    /// 分页查询订单列表
    /// </summary>
    [HttpGet("list")]
    [Authorize(Roles = "OrderStaff,OrderDirector,Admin")]

    {
        var result = await _orderService.GetPagedAsync(query);
        return Ok(ApiResponse<PagedResult<SalesOrderListDto>>.Ok(result, "查询成功"));
    }

    /// <summary>
    /// 根据ID获取订单详情
    /// </summary>
    [HttpGet("{id}")]
    [Authorize(Roles = "OrderStaff,OrderDirector,Admin")]
    public async Task<ActionResult<ApiResponse<SalesOrderDetailDto>>> GetById(int id)
    {
        var result = await _orderService.GetByIdAsync(id);
        return Ok(ApiResponse<SalesOrderDetailDto>.Ok(result, "查询成功"));
    }

    /// <summary>
    /// 创建订单
    /// </summary>
    [HttpPost]
    [Authorize(Roles = "OrderDirector,Admin")]
    public async Task<ActionResult<ApiResponse<SalesOrderListDto>>> Create([FromBody] CreateSalesOrderRequest request)
    {
        if (!ModelState.IsValid)
        {
            return BadRequest(ApiResponse<SalesOrderListDto>.Fail("请求参数无效"));
        }

        var result = await _orderService.CreateAsync(request);
        return Ok(ApiResponse<SalesOrderListDto>.Ok(result, "创建成功"));
    }

    /// <summary>
    /// 更新订单
    /// </summary>
    [HttpPut("{id}")]
    [Authorize(Roles = "OrderDirector,Admin")]
    public async Task<ActionResult<ApiResponse<SalesOrderListDto>>> Update(int id, [FromBody] UpdateSalesOrderRequest request)
    {
        var result = await _orderService.UpdateAsync(id, request);
        return Ok(ApiResponse<SalesOrderListDto>.Ok(result, "更新成功"));
    }

    /// <summary>
    /// 删除订单（软删除）
    /// </summary>
    [HttpDelete("{id}")]
    [Authorize(Roles = "OrderDirector,Admin")]
    public async Task<ActionResult<ApiResponse<object>>> Delete(int id)
    {
        await _orderService.DeleteAsync(id);
        return Ok(ApiResponse.Ok("删除成功"));
    }
}

FILE: MES.Api\Middlewares\ExceptionMiddleware.cs
======================================================================

using System.Text.Json;
using MES.Core.Models;
using MES.Core.Exceptions;

namespace MES.Api.Middlewares;

/// <summary>
/// 全局异常处理中间件
/// </summary>
public class ExceptionMiddleware
{
    private readonly RequestDelegate _next;
    private readonly ILogger<ExceptionMiddleware> _logger;

    public ExceptionMiddleware(RequestDelegate next, ILogger<ExceptionMiddleware> logger)
    {
        _next = next;
        _logger = logger;
    }

    public async Task InvokeAsync(HttpContext context)
    {
        try
        {
            await _next(context);
        }
        catch (BusinessException ex)
        {
            await HandleBusinessExceptionAsync(context, ex);
        }
        catch (UnauthorizedAccessException)
        {
            await HandleUnauthorizedExceptionAsync(context);
        }
        catch (Exception ex)
        {
            await HandleSystemExceptionAsync(context, ex);
        }
    }

    private async Task HandleBusinessExceptionAsync(HttpContext context, BusinessException ex)
    {
        context.Response.StatusCode = ex.Code;
        context.Response.ContentType = "application/json";

        var response = new ApiResponse<object>
        {
            Success = false,
            Code = ex.Code,
            Message = ex.Message
        };

        var result = JsonSerializer.Serialize(response, new JsonSerializerOptions
        {
            PropertyNamingPolicy = JsonNamingPolicy.CamelCase
        });

        await context.Response.WriteAsync(result);
    }

    private async Task HandleUnauthorizedExceptionAsync(HttpContext context)
    {
        context.Response.StatusCode = 401;
        context.Response.ContentType = "application/json";

        var response = new ApiResponse<object>
        {
            Success = false,
            Code = 401,
            Message = "未授权访问"
        };

        var result = JsonSerializer.Serialize(response, new JsonSerializerOptions
        {
            PropertyNamingPolicy = JsonNamingPolicy.CamelCase
        });

        await context.Response.WriteAsync(result);
    }

    private async Task HandleSystemExceptionAsync(HttpContext context, Exception ex)
    {
        _logger.LogError(ex, "系统异常: {Message}", ex.Message);

        context.Response.StatusCode = 500;
        context.Response.ContentType = "application/json";

        var response = new ApiResponse<object>
        {
            Success = false,
            Code = 500,
            Message = "系统内部错误，请稍后重试"
        };

#if DEBUG
        response.Message = ex.Message;
#endif

        var result = JsonSerializer.Serialize(response, new JsonSerializerOptions
        {
            PropertyNamingPolicy = JsonNamingPolicy.CamelCase
        });

        await context.Response.WriteAsync(result);
    }
}

/// <summary>
/// 全局异常处理中间件扩展方法
/// </summary>
public static class ExceptionMiddlewareExtensions
{
    public static IApplicationBuilder UseGlobalExceptionHandler(this IApplicationBuilder builder)
    {
        return builder.UseMiddleware<ExceptionMiddleware>();
    }
}

FILE: MES.Api\Program.cs

using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Authentication.JwtBearer;
using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Identity;
using Microsoft.EntityFrameworkCore;
using Microsoft.IdentityModel.Tokens;
using Microsoft.OpenApi.Models;
using System.Text;
using MES.Data;
using MES.Data.Entities;
using MES.Data.Seed;
using MES.Shared.Settings;
using MES.Auth.Services;
using MES.Api.Middlewares;
using MES.Core.Interfaces;
using MES.Services.Order;
using MES.Services;

var builder = WebApplication.CreateBuilder(args);

builder.Services.Configure<JwtSettings>(builder.Configuration.GetSection("JwtSettings"));
var jwtSettings = builder.Configuration.GetSection("JwtSettings").Get<JwtSettings>();

builder.Services.AddDbContext<AppDbContext>(options =>
    options.UseSqlServer(builder.Configuration.GetConnectionString("Default")));

builder.Services.AddIdentity<AppUser, IdentityRole>()
    .AddEntityFrameworkStores<AppDbContext>()
    .AddDefaultTokenProviders();

builder.Services.AddAuthentication(options =>
{
    options.DefaultAuthenticateScheme = JwtBearerDefaults.AuthenticationScheme;
    options.DefaultChallengeScheme = JwtBearerDefaults.AuthenticationScheme;
})
.AddJwtBearer(options =>
{
    options.TokenValidationParameters = new TokenValidationParameters
    {
        ValidateIssuer = true,
        ValidateAudience = true,
        ValidateLifetime = true,
        ValidateIssuerSigningKey = true,
        ValidIssuer = jwtSettings?.Issuer,
        ValidAudience = jwtSettings?.Audience,
        IssuerSigningKey = new SymmetricSecurityKey(Encoding.UTF8.GetBytes(jwtSettings?.Secret ?? ""))
    };
});

builder.Services.AddAuthorization();
builder.Services.AddControllers();
builder.Services.AddEndpointsApiExplorer();

// Swagger 配置（支持 JWT 认证）
builder.Services.AddSwaggerGen(c =>
{
    c.SwaggerDoc("v1", new OpenApiInfo
    {
        Title = "MES API",
        Version = "v1",
        Description = "MES 制造执行系统 API"
    });

    // 添加 JWT 认证配置
    c.AddSecurityDefinition("Bearer", new OpenApiSecurityScheme
    {
        Name = "Authorization",
        Type = SecuritySchemeType.ApiKey,
        Scheme = "Bearer",
        BearerFormat = "JWT",
        In = ParameterLocation.Header,
        Description = "请输入 JWT Token，格式：Bearer {your token}"
    });

    c.AddSecurityRequirement(new OpenApiSecurityRequirement
    {
        {
            new OpenApiSecurityScheme
            {
                Reference = new OpenApiReference
                {
                    Type = ReferenceType.SecurityScheme,
                    Id = "Bearer"
                }
            },
            new string[] {}
        }
    });
});

// 注册认证服务
builder.Services.AddScoped<IAuthService, AuthService>();
builder.Services.AddScoped<IJwtService, JwtService>();

// 注册订单服务
builder.Services.AddScoped<IOrderService, OrderService>();

// 注册辅助服务
builder.Services.AddScoped<ICustomerService, CustomerService>();
builder.Services.AddScoped<IProductionStandardService, ProductionStandardService>();
builder.Services.AddScoped<IGradeMappingService, GradeMappingService>();

builder.Services.AddHttpContextAccessor();

builder.Services.AddCors(options =>
{
    options.AddPolicy("AllowBlazor", policy =>
    {
        policy.WithOrigins("https://localhost:5001", "http://localhost:5000")
              .AllowAnyHeader()
              .AllowAnyMethod()
              .AllowCredentials();
    });
});

var app = builder.Build();

using (var scope = app.Services.CreateScope())
{
    await DbInitializer.InitializeAsync(scope.ServiceProvider);
}

if (app.Environment.IsDevelopment())
{
    app.UseSwagger();
    app.UseSwaggerUI();
}

app.UseHttpsRedirection();
app.UseCors("AllowBlazor");

// 使用自定义中间件
app.UseMiddleware<ExceptionMiddleware>();

app.UseAuthentication();
app.UseAuthorization();
app.MapControllers();
app.Run();

FILE: MES.Auth\Services\AuthService.cs

// 文件路径: MES.Auth/Services/AuthService.cs
using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Identity;
using Microsoft.Extensions.Configuration;
using Microsoft.IdentityModel.Tokens;
using System.IdentityModel.Tokens.Jwt;
using System.Security.Claims;
using System.Text;
using MES.Data.Entities;
using MES.Core.DTOs.Auth;
using MES.Core.Models;
using MES.Data;
using MES.Shared.Settings;

namespace MES.Auth.Services;

/// <summary>
/// 认证服务实现
/// </summary>
public class AuthService : IAuthService
{
    private readonly UserManager<AppUser> _userManager;
    private readonly SignInManager<AppUser> _signInManager;
    private readonly IConfiguration _configuration;
    private readonly IJwtService _jwtService;
    private readonly AppDbContext _context;

    public AuthService(
        UserManager<AppUser> userManager,
        SignInManager<AppUser> signInManager,
        IConfiguration configuration,
        IJwtService jwtService,
        AppDbContext context)
    {
        _userManager = userManager;
        _signInManager = signInManager;
        _configuration = configuration;
        _jwtService = jwtService;
        _context = context;
    }

    /// <summary>
    /// 用户登录
    /// </summary>
    public async Task<ApiResponse<LoginResponse>> LoginAsync(LoginRequest request)
    {
        // 参数验证
        if (string.IsNullOrEmpty(request.Email))
        {
            return ApiResponse<LoginResponse>.Fail("邮箱不能为空");
        }

        if (string.IsNullOrEmpty(request.Password))
        {
            return ApiResponse<LoginResponse>.Fail("密码不能为空");
        }

        // 查找用户
        var user = await _userManager.FindByEmailAsync(request.Email);
        if (user == null)
        {
            return ApiResponse<LoginResponse>.Fail("用户名或密码错误");
        }

        // 验证密码
        var result = await _signInManager.CheckPasswordSignInAsync(user, request.Password, false);
        if (!result.Succeeded)
        {
            return ApiResponse<LoginResponse>.Fail("用户名或密码错误");
        }

        // 检查用户状态
        if (!user.IsActive)
        {
            return ApiResponse<LoginResponse>.Fail("用户账户已被禁用，请联系管理员");
        }

        // 获取用户角色
        var roles = await _userManager.GetRolesAsync(user);

        // 生成JWT令牌
        var token = await _jwtService.GenerateTokenAsync(user, roles);

        // 更新最后登录时间
        user.LastLoginAt = DateTime.UtcNow;
        await _userManager.UpdateAsync(user);

        // 获取JWT配置
        var jwtSettings = _configuration.GetSection("JwtSettings").Get<JwtSettings>();

        // 返回登录响应 - 使用 null 合并运算符处理可能的 null 值
        var loginResponse = new LoginResponse
        {
            Token = token,
            Email = user.Email ?? string.Empty,      // 修复 CS8601
            UserName = user.UserName ?? string.Empty, // 修复 CS8601
            Roles = roles.ToList(),
            Expires = DateTime.UtcNow.AddMinutes(jwtSettings?.ExpireMinutes ?? 480),
            FullName = user.FullName ?? string.Empty  // 修复 CS8601
        };

        return ApiResponse<LoginResponse>.Ok(loginResponse);
    }

    /// <summary>
    /// 获取当前用户信息
    /// </summary>
    public async Task<ApiResponse<UserInfoResponse>> GetCurrentUserAsync()
    {
        // TODO: 从 HttpContext 获取当前用户
        // 这里返回一个占位响应，避免 CS1998 警告
        await Task.CompletedTask;  // 修复 CS1998 - 添加真正的异步等待

        return ApiResponse<UserInfoResponse>.Fail("获取当前用户信息功能待实现");
    }

    /// <summary>
    /// 注销登录
    /// </summary>
    public async Task<ApiResponse<object>> LogoutAsync()
    {
        await _signInManager.SignOutAsync();
        // 使用 ApiResponse<object>.Ok 并传入一个空对象或字符串
        return ApiResponse<object>.Ok(new object(), "注销成功");
    }

    /// <summary>
    /// 刷新令牌
    /// </summary>
    public async Task<ApiResponse<LoginResponse>> RefreshTokenAsync(string refreshToken)
    {
        // 参数验证 - 修复 CS8625
        if (string.IsNullOrEmpty(refreshToken))
        {
            return ApiResponse<LoginResponse>.Fail("刷新令牌不能为空");
        }

        // TODO: 实现刷新令牌逻辑
        await Task.CompletedTask;  // 添加真正的异步等待

        return ApiResponse<LoginResponse>.Fail("刷新令牌功能待实现");
    }
}

/// <summary>
/// JWT服务实现
/// </summary>
public class JwtService : IJwtService
{
    private readonly IConfiguration _configuration;
    private readonly UserManager<AppUser> _userManager;

    public JwtService(IConfiguration configuration, UserManager<AppUser> userManager)
    {
        _configuration = configuration;
        _userManager = userManager;
    }

    public Task<string> GenerateTokenAsync(AppUser user, IList<string> roles)
    {
        var jwtSettings = _configuration.GetSection("JwtSettings").Get<JwtSettings>();
        if (jwtSettings == null)
        {
            throw new InvalidOperationException("JWT配置未找到");
        }

        var key = new SymmetricSecurityKey(Encoding.UTF8.GetBytes(jwtSettings.Secret));
        var creds = new SigningCredentials(key, SecurityAlgorithms.HmacSha256);

        // 修复 CS8604 - 使用 null 合并运算符确保非空
        var userId = user.Id ?? throw new InvalidOperationException("用户ID不能为空");
        var userEmail = user.Email ?? throw new InvalidOperationException("用户邮箱不能为空");
        var userName = user.UserName ?? throw new InvalidOperationException("用户名不能为空");
        var fullName = user.FullName ?? string.Empty;

        var claims = new List<Claim>
        {
            new Claim(JwtRegisteredClaimNames.Sub, userId),
            new Claim(JwtRegisteredClaimNames.Email, userEmail),
            new Claim(JwtRegisteredClaimNames.Name, userName),
            new Claim(JwtRegisteredClaimNames.Jti, Guid.NewGuid().ToString()),
            new Claim("fullName", fullName)
        };

        // 添加角色声明
        foreach (var role in roles)
        {
            claims.Add(new Claim(ClaimTypes.Role, role));
        }

        var token = new JwtSecurityToken(
            issuer: jwtSettings.Issuer,
            audience: jwtSettings.Audience,
            claims: claims,
            expires: DateTime.UtcNow.AddMinutes(jwtSettings.ExpireMinutes),
            signingCredentials: creds
        );

        return Task.FromResult(new JwtSecurityTokenHandler().WriteToken(token));
    }

    public string GetUsernameFromToken(string token)
    {
        if (string.IsNullOrEmpty(token))
        {
            return string.Empty;
        }

        try
        {
            var tokenHandler = new JwtSecurityTokenHandler();
            var jwtToken = tokenHandler.ReadToken(token) as JwtSecurityToken;
            return jwtToken?.Claims.FirstOrDefault(c => c.Type == JwtRegisteredClaimNames.Name)?.Value ?? string.Empty;
        }
        catch
        {
            return string.Empty;
        }
    }

    public bool ValidateToken(string token)
    {
        if (string.IsNullOrEmpty(token))
        {
            return false;
        }

        try
        {
            var jwtSettings = _configuration.GetSection("JwtSettings").Get<JwtSettings>();
            if (jwtSettings == null)
                return false;

            var tokenHandler = new JwtSecurityTokenHandler();
            var key = Encoding.UTF8.GetBytes(jwtSettings.Secret);

            tokenHandler.ValidateToken(token, new TokenValidationParameters
            {
                ValidateIssuerSigningKey = true,
                IssuerSigningKey = new SymmetricSecurityKey(key),
                ValidateIssuer = true,
                ValidIssuer = jwtSettings.Issuer,
                ValidateAudience = true,
                ValidAudience = jwtSettings.Audience,
                ValidateLifetime = true,
                ClockSkew = TimeSpan.Zero
            }, out SecurityToken validatedToken);

            return true;
        }
        catch
        {
            return false;
        }
    }
}

FILE: MES.Auth\Services\IAuthService.cs

using MES.Data.Entities;
using MES.Core.DTOs.Auth;
using MES.Core.Models;

namespace MES.Auth.Services;

/// <summary>
/// 认证服务接口
/// </summary>
public interface IAuthService
{
    /// <summary>
    /// 用户登录
    /// </summary>
    /// <param name="request">登录请求</param>
    /// <returns>登录响应</returns>
    Task<ApiResponse<LoginResponse>> LoginAsync(LoginRequest request);

    /// <summary>
    /// 注销登录
    /// </summary>
    /// <returns>注销结果</returns>
    Task<ApiResponse<object>> LogoutAsync();

    /// <summary>
    /// 刷新令牌
    /// </summary>
    /// <param name="refreshToken">刷新令牌</param>
    /// <returns>新的令牌响应</returns>
    Task<ApiResponse<LoginResponse>> RefreshTokenAsync(string refreshToken);

    /// <summary>
    /// 获取当前用户信息
    /// </summary>
    /// <returns>用户信息</returns>
    Task<ApiResponse<UserInfoResponse>> GetCurrentUserAsync();
}

/// <summary>
/// JWT令牌服务接口
/// </summary>
public interface IJwtService
{
    /// <summary>
    /// 生成JWT令牌
    /// </summary>
    /// <param name="user">用户信息</param>
    /// <param name="roles">角色列表</param>
    /// <returns>JWT令牌</returns>
    Task<string> GenerateTokenAsync(AppUser user, IList<string> roles);

    /// <summary>
    /// 从令牌中获取用户名
    /// </summary>
    /// <param name="token">JWT令牌</param>
    /// <returns>用户名</returns>
    string GetUsernameFromToken(string token);

    /// <summary>
    /// 验证令牌有效性
    /// </summary>
    /// <param name="token">JWT令牌</param>
    /// <returns>是否有效</returns>
    bool ValidateToken(string token);
}

/// <summary>
/// 登录请求DTO
/// </summary>
public class LoginRequest
{
    public string Email { get; set; } = string.Empty;
    public string Password { get; set; } = string.Empty;
}

/// <summary>
/// 用户信息响应DTO
/// </summary>
public class UserInfoResponse
{
    public string UserId { get; set; } = string.Empty;
    public string Email { get; set; } = string.Empty;
    public string UserName { get; set; } = string.Empty;
    public List<string> Roles { get; set; } = new();
}

@page "/customers/create"
@using MES.Blazor.Services
@using MES.Core.DTOs
@using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Authorization
@inject ICustomerService CustomerService
@inject NavigationManager Navigation
@inject ISnackbar Snackbar
@attribute [Authorize(Roles = "OrderDirector,Admin")]

<MudContainer MaxWidth="MaxWidth.Large" Class="mt-4">
    <MudCard>
        <MudCardHeader>
            <CardHeaderContent>
                <MudText Typo="Typo.h5" Class="font-weight-bold">
                    <MudIcon Icon="@Icons.Material.Filled.Add" Class="mr-2" Color="Color.Primary" />
                    新建客户
                </MudText>
                <MudText Typo="Typo.body2" Color="Color.Secondary">创建新的客户档案</MudText>
            </CardHeaderContent>
            <CardHeaderActions>
                <MudButton Variant="Variant.Text" OnClick="GoBack">返回</MudButton>
                <MudButton Variant="Variant.Filled" Color="Color.Primary" OnClick="SaveCustomer" Disabled="@isSubmitting">
                    @if (isSubmitting)
                    {
                        <MudProgressCircular Size="Size.Small" Color="Color.Inherit" />
                    }
                    else
                    {
                        <span>保存</span>
                    }
                </MudButton>
            </CardHeaderActions>
        </MudCardHeader>

        <MudCardContent>
            <MudGrid>
                <MudItem xs="12" md="6">
                    <MudTextField T="string" 
                                  Label="客户编码" 
                                  @bind-Value="customer.CustomerCode" 
                                  Required="true" />
                </MudItem>
                <MudItem xs="12" md="6">
                    <MudTextField T="string" 
                                  Label="业务员" 
                                  @bind-Value="customer.Salesman" 
                                  Required="true" />
                </MudItem>
                <MudItem xs="12" md="12">
                    <MudTextField T="string" 
                                  Label="客户单位" 
                                  @bind-Value="customer.CustomerUnit" 
                                  Required="true" />
                </MudItem>
                <MudItem xs="12" md="6">
                    <MudTextField T="string" 
                                  Label="最终用户" 
                                  @bind-Value="customer.EndCustomer" />
                </MudItem>
                <MudItem xs="12" md="6">
                    <MudSelect T="string" Label="状态" @bind-Value="customer.Status">
                        <MudSelectItem Value="@("Active")">启用</MudSelectItem>
                        <MudSelectItem Value="@("Inactive")">停用</MudSelectItem>
                    </MudSelect>
                </MudItem>
                <MudItem xs="12" md="6">
                    <MudTextField T="string" 
                                  Label="联系人" 
                                  @bind-Value="customer.ContactPerson" />
                </MudItem>
                <MudItem xs="12" md="6">
                    <MudTextField T="string" 
                                  Label="联系电话" 
                                  @bind-Value="customer.ContactPhone" />
                </MudItem>
                <MudItem xs="12" md="12">
                    <MudTextField T="string" 
                                  Label="联系地址" 
                                  @bind-Value="customer.Address" />
                </MudItem>
                <MudItem xs="12" md="12">
                    <MudTextField T="string" 
                                  Label="备注" 
                                  @bind-Value="customer.Remark" 
                                  Multiline="true" />
                </MudItem>
            </MudGrid>
        </MudCardContent>
    </MudCard>
</MudContainer>

@code {
    private CreateCustomerRequest customer = new() { Status = "Active" };
    private bool isSubmitting;

    private async Task SaveCustomer()
    {
        if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(customer.CustomerCode))
        {
            Snackbar.Add("客户编码不能为空", Severity.Warning);
            return;
        }

        if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(customer.Salesman))
        {
            Snackbar.Add("业务员不能为空", Severity.Warning);
            return;
        }

        if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(customer.CustomerUnit))
        {
            Snackbar.Add("客户单位不能为空", Severity.Warning);
            return;
        }

        isSubmitting = true;
        StateHasChanged();

        var result = await CustomerService.CreateAsync(customer);
        if (result.Success)
        {
            Snackbar.Add("创建成功", Severity.Success);
            Navigation.NavigateTo("/customers");
        }
        else
        {
            Snackbar.Add(result.Message ?? "创建失败", Severity.Error);
        }

        isSubmitting = false;
        StateHasChanged();
    }

    private void GoBack()
    {
        Navigation.NavigateTo("/customers");
    }
}

@page "/customers/{id:int}"
@page "/customers/{id:int}/edit"
@using MES.Blazor.Services
@using MES.Core.DTOs
@using MES.Core.Enums
@using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Authorization
@inject ICustomerService CustomerService
@inject NavigationManager Navigation
@inject ISnackbar Snackbar
@attribute [Authorize(Roles = "OrderStaff,OrderDirector,Admin")]

<MudContainer MaxWidth="MaxWidth.Large" Class="mt-4">
    @if (isLoading)
    {
        <MudProgressCircular Indeterminate Size="Size.Large" Class="d-flex justify-center ma-8" />
    }
    else if (customer == null)
    {
        <MudAlert Severity="Severity.Error">客户不存在</MudAlert>
    }
    else
    {
        <MudCard>
            <MudCardHeader>
                <CardHeaderContent>
                    <MudText Typo="Typo.h5" Class="font-weight-bold">
                        <MudIcon Icon="@Icons.Material.Filled.Business" Class="mr-2" Color="Color.Primary" />
                        客户详情
                    </MudText>
                    <MudText Typo="Typo.body2" Color="Color.Secondary">
                        客户编码：@customer.CustomerCode
                    </MudText>
                </CardHeaderContent>
                <CardHeaderActions>
                    <MudButton Variant="Variant.Text" OnClick="GoBack">返回</MudButton>
                    @if (isEditMode)
                    {
                        <MudButton Variant="Variant.Filled" Color="Color.Primary" OnClick="SaveCustomer" Disabled="@isSubmitting">
                            @if (isSubmitting)
                            {
                                <MudProgressCircular Size="Size.Small" Color="Color.Inherit" />
                            }
                            else
                            {
                                <span>保存</span>
                            }
                        </MudButton>
                    }
                    else
                    {
                        <AuthorizeView Roles="OrderDirector,Admin">
                            <MudButton Variant="Variant.Outlined" Color="Color.Warning" OnClick="EnterEditMode">编辑</MudButton>
                        </AuthorizeView>
                    }
                </CardHeaderActions>
            </MudCardHeader>

            <MudCardContent>
                <MudGrid>
                    <MudItem xs="12" md="6">
                        <MudTextField T="string"
                                      Label="客户编码"
                                      @bind-Value="editCustomer.CustomerCode"
                                      Disabled="!isEditMode"
                                      Required="true"
                                      HelperText="唯一标识，不可重复" />
                    </MudItem>
                    <MudItem xs="12" md="6">
                        <MudTextField T="string"
                                      Label="业务员"
                                      @bind-Value="editCustomer.Salesman"
                                      Disabled="!isEditMode"
                                      Required="true" />
                    </MudItem>
                    <MudItem xs="12" md="12">
                        <MudTextField T="string"
                                      Label="客户单位"
                                      @bind-Value="editCustomer.CustomerUnit"
                                      Disabled="!isEditMode"
                                      Required="true" />
                    </MudItem>
                    <MudItem xs="12" md="6">
                        <MudTextField T="string"
                                      Label="最终用户"
                                      @bind-Value="editCustomer.EndCustomer"
                                      Disabled="!isEditMode" />
                    </MudItem>
                    <MudItem xs="12" md="6">
                        <MudSelect T="CustomerStatus?"
                                   Label="状态"
                                   @bind-Value="editCustomer.Status"
                                   Disabled="!isEditMode"
                                   Required="true">
                            <MudSelectItem Value="@CustomerStatus.Active">启用</MudSelectItem>
                            <MudSelectItem Value="@CustomerStatus.Inactive">停用</MudSelectItem>
                        </MudSelect>
                    </MudItem>
                    <MudItem xs="12" md="6">
                        <MudTextField T="string"
                                      Label="联系人"
                                      @bind-Value="editCustomer.ContactPerson"
                                      Disabled="!isEditMode" />
                    </MudItem>
                    <MudItem xs="12" md="6">
                        <MudTextField T="string"
                                      Label="联系电话"
                                      @bind-Value="editCustomer.ContactPhone"
                                      Disabled="!isEditMode" />
                    </MudItem>
                    <MudItem xs="12" md="12">
                        <MudTextField T="string"
                                      Label="联系地址"
                                      @bind-Value="editCustomer.Address"
                                      Disabled="!isEditMode"
                                      Multiline="true"
                                      Lines="2" />
                    </MudItem>
                    <MudItem xs="12" md="12">
                        <MudTextField T="string"
                                      Label="备注"
                                      @bind-Value="editCustomer.Remark"
                                      Disabled="!isEditMode"
                                      Multiline="true"
                                      Lines="3" />
                    </MudItem>
                </MudGrid>
            </MudCardContent>
        </MudCard>
    }
</MudContainer>

@code {
    [Parameter] public int Id { get; set; }

    private bool isEditMode => Navigation.Uri.Contains("/edit");
    private CustomerProfileDto? customer;
    private UpdateCustomerRequest editCustomer = new();
    private bool isLoading = true;
    private bool isSubmitting;

    protected override async Task OnInitializedAsync()
    {
        await LoadData();
    }

    private async Task LoadData()
    {
        isLoading = true;
        StateHasChanged();

        var result = await CustomerService.GetByIdAsync(Id);
        if (result.Success && result.Data != null)
        {
            customer = result.Data;

            // 将字符串状态转换为枚举
            var status = customer.Status switch
            {
                "Active" => CustomerStatus.Active,
                "Inactive" => CustomerStatus.Inactive,
                _ => CustomerStatus.Active
            };

            editCustomer = new UpdateCustomerRequest
            {
                CustomerCode = customer.CustomerCode,
                Salesman = customer.Salesman,
                CustomerUnit = customer.CustomerUnit,
                EndCustomer = customer.EndCustomer,
                ContactPerson = customer.ContactPerson,
                ContactPhone = customer.ContactPhone,
                Address = customer.Address,
                Status = status,
                Remark = customer.Remark
            };
        }

        isLoading = false;
        StateHasChanged();
    }

    private void EnterEditMode()
    {
        Navigation.NavigateTo($"/customers/{Id}/edit");
    }

    private async Task SaveCustomer()
    {
        // 验证必填字段
        if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(editCustomer.CustomerCode))
        {
            Snackbar.Add("客户编码不能为空", Severity.Warning);
            return;
        }

        if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(editCustomer.Salesman))
        {
            Snackbar.Add("业务员不能为空", Severity.Warning);
            return;
        }

        if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(editCustomer.CustomerUnit))
        {
            Snackbar.Add("客户单位不能为空", Severity.Warning);
            return;
        }

        // 验证状态
        if (!editCustomer.Status.HasValue)
        {
            Snackbar.Add("请选择客户状态", Severity.Warning);
            return;
        }

        isSubmitting = true;
        StateHasChanged();

        var result = await CustomerService.UpdateAsync(Id, editCustomer);
        if (result.Success)
        {
            Snackbar.Add("更新成功", Severity.Success);
            Navigation.NavigateTo($"/customers/{Id}");
        }
        else
        {
            Snackbar.Add(result.Message ?? "更新失败", Severity.Error);
        }

        isSubmitting = false;
        StateHasChanged();
    }

    private void GoBack()
    {
        Navigation.NavigateTo("/customers");
    }
}

@page "/customers"
@using MES.Blazor.Services
@using MES.Core.DTOs
@using MES.Core.Models
@using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Authorization
@inject ICustomerService CustomerService
@inject NavigationManager Navigation
@inject ISnackbar Snackbar
@inject IDialogService DialogService
@attribute [Authorize(Roles = "OrderStaff,OrderDirector,Admin")]

<MudContainer MaxWidth="MaxWidth.Large" Class="mt-4">
    <MudCard>
        <MudCardHeader>
            <CardHeaderContent>
                <MudText Typo="Typo.h5" Class="font-weight-bold">
                    <MudIcon Icon="@Icons.Material.Filled.Business" Class="mr-2" Color="Color.Primary" />
                    客户管理
                </MudText>
                <MudText Typo="Typo.body2" Color="Color.Secondary">客户档案信息</MudText>
            </CardHeaderContent>
            <CardHeaderActions>
                <MudButton Variant="Variant.Filled" 
                           Color="Color.Primary" 
                           StartIcon="@Icons.Material.Filled.Add"
                           OnClick="NavigateToCreate">
                    新建客户
                </MudButton>
            </CardHeaderActions>
        </MudCardHeader>

        <MudCardContent>
            <!-- 搜索栏 -->
            <MudGrid>
                <MudItem xs="12" md="8">
                    <MudTextField T="string"
                                  Label="搜索客户编码/单位/业务员"
                                  Immediate="true"
                                  Adornment="Adornment.End"
                                  AdornmentIcon="@Icons.Material.Filled.Search"
                                  @bind-Value="searchKeyword"
                                  @bind-Value:event="oninput"
                                  OnKeyDown="OnSearchKeyDown" />
                </MudItem>
                <MudItem xs="12" md="4">
                    <MudButton Variant="Variant.Outlined" 
                               Color="Color.Primary" 
                               FullWidth="true"
                               OnClick="Search">
                        搜索
                    </MudButton>
                </MudItem>
            </MudGrid>

            <!-- 表格 -->
            <MudTable Items="@customers" Loading="@isLoading" Dense="true" Hover="true" Breakpoint="Breakpoint.Sm" Class="mt-4">
                <HeaderContent>
                    <MudTh>客户编码</MudTh>
                    <MudTh>客户单位</MudTh>
                    <MudTh>业务员</MudTh>
                    <MudTh>联系人</MudTh>
                    <MudTh>联系电话</MudTh>
                    <MudTh>状态</MudTh>
                    <MudTh>操作</MudTh>
                </HeaderContent>
                <RowTemplate>
                    <MudTd>@context.CustomerCode</MudTd>
                    <MudTd>@context.CustomerUnit</MudTd>
                    <MudTd>@context.Salesman</MudTd>
                    <MudTd>@context.ContactPerson</MudTd>
                    <MudTd>@context.ContactPhone</MudTd>
                    <MudTd>
                        <MudChip Size="Size.Small" Color="@(context.Status == "Active" ? Color.Success : Color.Error)">
                            @(context.Status == "Active" ? "启用" : "停用")
                        </MudChip>
                    </MudTd>
                    <MudTd>
                        <MudButton Variant="Variant.Text" Size="Size.Small" Color="Color.Info" OnClick="() => ViewCustomer(context.Id)">查看</MudButton>
                        <MudButton Variant="Variant.Text" Size="Size.Small" Color="Color.Warning" OnClick="() => EditCustomer(context.Id)">编辑</MudButton>
                        <MudButton Variant="Variant.Text" Size="Size.Small" Color="Color.Error" OnClick="() => DeleteCustomer(context.Id)">删除</MudButton>
                    </MudTd>
                </RowTemplate>
                <PagerContent>
                    <MudTablePager />
                </PagerContent>
            </MudTable>
        </MudCardContent>
    </MudCard>
</MudContainer>

@code {
    private List<CustomerProfileDto> customers = new();
    private int totalCount;
    private bool isLoading = true;
    private string searchKeyword = string.Empty;
    private QueryParams queryParams = new() { PageSize = 20 };

    protected override async Task OnInitializedAsync()
    {
        await LoadData();
    }

    private async Task LoadData()
    {
        isLoading = true;
        StateHasChanged();

        queryParams.Keyword = searchKeyword;
        var result = await CustomerService.GetPagedAsync(queryParams);

        if (result.Success && result.Data != null)
        {
            customers = result.Data.Items;
            totalCount = result.Data.TotalCount;
        }
        else
        {
            Snackbar.Add(result.Message ?? "加载数据失败", Severity.Error);
        }

        isLoading = false;
        StateHasChanged();
    }

    private async Task Search()
    {
        queryParams.PageIndex = 1;
        await LoadData();
    }

    private void OnSearchKeyDown(KeyboardEventArgs args)
    {
        if (args.Key == "Enter")
        {
            _ = Search();
        }
    }

    private void NavigateToCreate()
    {
        Navigation.NavigateTo("/customers/create");
    }

    private void ViewCustomer(int id)
    {
        Navigation.NavigateTo($"/customers/{id}");
    }

    private void EditCustomer(int id)
    {
        Navigation.NavigateTo($"/customers/{id}/edit");
    }

    private async Task DeleteCustomer(int id)
    {
        bool? confirmed = await DialogService.ShowMessageBox(
            "确认删除",
            "确定要删除该客户吗？",
            yesText: "删除", cancelText: "取消");

        if (confirmed == true)
        {
            var result = await CustomerService.DeleteAsync(id);
            if (result.Success)
            {
                Snackbar.Add("删除成功", Severity.Success);
                await LoadData();
            }
            else
            {
                Snackbar.Add(result.Message ?? "删除失败", Severity.Error);
            }
        }
    }
}

======================================================================
FILE: MES.Blazor\Pages\GradeMappingCreate.razor
======================================================================

@page "/grade-mappings/create"
@using MES.Blazor.Services
@using MES.Core.DTOs
@using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Authorization
@using MudBlazor
@inject IGradeMappingService GradeMappingService
@inject NavigationManager Navigation
@inject ISnackbar Snackbar
@attribute [Authorize(Roles = "OrderDirector,Admin")]

<MudContainer MaxWidth="MaxWidth.Large" Class="mt-4">
    <MudCard>
        <MudCardHeader>
            <CardHeaderContent>
                <MudText Typo="Typo.h5" Class="font-weight-bold">
                    <MudIcon Icon="@Icons.Material.Filled.Add" Class="mr-2" Color="Color.Primary" />
                    新建牌号对照
                </MudText>
                <MudText Typo="Typo.body2" Color="Color.Secondary">创建标准牌号与工厂牌号的映射</MudText>
            </CardHeaderContent>
            <CardHeaderActions>
                <MudButton Variant="Variant.Text" OnClick="GoBack">返回</MudButton>
                <MudButton Variant="Variant.Filled" Color="Color.Primary" OnClick="SaveGradeMapping" Disabled="@isSubmitting">
                    @if (isSubmitting)
                    {
                        <MudProgressCircular Size="Size.Small" Color="Color.Inherit" />
                    }
                    else
                    {
                        <span>保存</span>
                    }
                </MudButton>
            </CardHeaderActions>
        </MudCardHeader>

        <MudCardContent>
            <MudGrid>
                <MudItem xs="12" md="6">
                    <MudTextField T="string"
                                  Label="标准牌号"
                                  @bind-Value="gradeMapping.StandardGrade"
                                  Required="true"
                                  HelperText="如 304, 316L" />
                </MudItem>
                <MudItem xs="12" md="6">
                    <MudTextField T="string"
                                  Label="工厂牌号"
                                  @bind-Value="gradeMapping.PlantGrade"
                                  Required="true"
                                  HelperText="如 06Cr19Ni10" />
                </MudItem>
                <MudItem xs="12" md="6">
                    <MudNumericField T="decimal"
                                     Label="密度 (g/cm³)"
                                     @bind-Value="densityValue"
                                     Required="true"
                                     Format="F4"
                                     Min="0" />
                </MudItem>
                <MudItem xs="12" md="6">
                    <!-- 修复 CS0618: 使用 @bind-Value 替代 CheckedChanged -->
                    <MudSwitch @bind-Value="gradeMapping.SpecialMaterial" Label="特殊材料" />
                </MudItem>
                <MudItem xs="12" md="12">
                    <MudTextField T="string"
                                  Label="热处理工艺"
                                  @bind-Value="gradeMapping.HeatTreatment"
                                  HelperText="如：固溶处理 1010-1150℃，快冷" />
                </MudItem>
                <MudItem xs="12" md="12">
                    <MudTextField T="string"
                                  Label="特殊注意事项"
                                  @bind-Value="gradeMapping.SpecialNote"
                                  Style="min-height: 80px;" />
                </MudItem>
                <MudItem xs="12" md="12">
                    <MudTextField T="string"
                                  Label="备注"
                                  @bind-Value="gradeMapping.Remark"
                                  Style="min-height: 80px;" />
                </MudItem>
            </MudGrid>
        </MudCardContent>
    </MudCard>
</MudContainer>

@code {
    private CreateGradeMappingRequest gradeMapping = new() { Density = 7.93m, SpecialMaterial = false };
    private bool isSubmitting;

    // 用于绑定密度的局部变量
    private decimal densityValue = 7.93m;

    protected override void OnInitialized()
    {
        densityValue = gradeMapping.Density;
    }

    private async Task SaveGradeMapping()
    {
        if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(gradeMapping.StandardGrade))
        {
            Snackbar.Add("标准牌号不能为空", Severity.Warning);
            return;
        }

        if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(gradeMapping.PlantGrade))
        {
            Snackbar.Add("工厂牌号不能为空", Severity.Warning);
            return;
        }

        // 将局部变量赋值回 gradeMapping
        gradeMapping.Density = densityValue;

        if (gradeMapping.Density <= 0)
        {
            Snackbar.Add("密度必须大于0", Severity.Warning);
            return;
        }

        isSubmitting = true;
        StateHasChanged();

        var result = await GradeMappingService.CreateAsync(gradeMapping);
        if (result != null && result.Success)
        {
            Snackbar.Add("创建成功", Severity.Success);
            Navigation.NavigateTo("/grade-mappings");
        }
        else
        {
            Snackbar.Add(result?.Message ?? "创建失败", Severity.Error);
        }

        isSubmitting = false;
        StateHasChanged();
    }

    private void GoBack()
    {
        Navigation.NavigateTo("/grade-mappings");
    }
}

FILE: MES.Blazor\Pages\GradeMappingDetail.razor

@page "/grade-mappings/{id:int}"
@page "/grade-mappings/{id:int}/edit"
@using MES.Blazor.Services
@using MES.Core.DTOs
@using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Authorization
@using MudBlazor
@inject IGradeMappingService GradeMappingService
@inject NavigationManager Navigation
@inject ISnackbar Snackbar
@attribute [Authorize(Roles = "OrderStaff,OrderDirector,Admin")]

<MudContainer MaxWidth="MaxWidth.Large" Class="mt-4">
    @if (isLoading)
    {
        <MudProgressCircular Indeterminate Size="Size.Large" Class="d-flex justify-center ma-8" />
    }
    else if (gradeMapping == null)
    {
        <MudAlert Severity="Severity.Error">牌号对照不存在</MudAlert>
    }
    else
    {
        <MudCard>
            <MudCardHeader>
                <CardHeaderContent>
                    <MudText Typo="Typo.h5" Class="font-weight-bold">
                        <MudIcon Icon="@Icons.Material.Filled.Science" Class="mr-2" Color="Color.Primary" />
                        牌号对照详情
                    </MudText>
                    <MudText Typo="Typo.body2" Color="Color.Secondary">
                        标准牌号：@gradeMapping.StandardGrade
                    </MudText>
                </CardHeaderContent>
                <CardHeaderActions>
                    <MudButton Variant="Variant.Text" OnClick="GoBack">返回</MudButton>
                    @if (isEditMode)
                    {
                        <MudButton Variant="Variant.Filled" Color="Color.Primary" OnClick="SaveGradeMapping" Disabled="@isSubmitting">
                            @if (isSubmitting)
                            {
                                <MudProgressCircular Size="Size.Small" Color="Color.Inherit" />
                            }
                            else
                            {
                                <span>保存</span>
                            }
                        </MudButton>
                    }
                    else
                    {
                        <AuthorizeView Roles="OrderDirector,Admin">
                            <MudButton Variant="Variant.Outlined" Color="Color.Warning" OnClick="EnterEditMode">编辑</MudButton>
                        </AuthorizeView>
                    }
                </CardHeaderActions>
            </MudCardHeader>

            <MudCardContent>
                <MudGrid>
                    <MudItem xs="12" md="6">
                        <MudTextField T="string"
                                      Label="标准牌号"
                                      @bind-Value="editGrade.StandardGrade"
                                      Disabled="!isEditMode"
                                      HelperText="如 304, 316L" />
                    </MudItem>
                    <MudItem xs="12" md="6">
                        <MudTextField T="string"
                                      Label="工厂牌号"
                                      @bind-Value="editGrade.PlantGrade"
                                      Disabled="!isEditMode"
                                      HelperText="如 06Cr19Ni10" />
                    </MudItem>
                    <MudItem xs="12" md="6">
                        <MudNumericField T="decimal"
                                         Label="密度 (g/cm³)"
                                         @bind-Value="densityValue"
                                         Disabled="!isEditMode"
                                         Format="F4"
                                         Min="0" />
                    </MudItem>
                    <MudItem xs="12" md="6">
                        <!-- 修复 CS0618: 使用 @bind-Value 替代 CheckedChanged -->
                        <MudSwitch @bind-Value="editGrade.SpecialMaterial" Label="特殊材料" Disabled="!isEditMode" />
                    </MudItem>
                    <MudItem xs="12" md="12">
                        <MudTextField T="string"
                                      Label="热处理工艺"
                                      @bind-Value="editGrade.HeatTreatment"
                                      Disabled="!isEditMode"
                                      HelperText="如：固溶处理 1010-1150℃，快冷" />
                    </MudItem>
                    <MudItem xs="12" md="12">
                        <MudTextField T="string"
                                      Label="特殊注意事项"
                                      @bind-Value="editGrade.SpecialNote"
                                      Disabled="!isEditMode"
                                      Style="min-height: 80px;" />
                    </MudItem>
                    <MudItem xs="12" md="12">
                        <MudTextField T="string"
                                      Label="备注"
                                      @bind-Value="editGrade.Remark"
                                      Disabled="!isEditMode"
                                      Style="min-height: 80px;" />
                    </MudItem>
                </MudGrid>
            </MudCardContent>
        </MudCard>
    }
</MudContainer>

@code {
    [Parameter] public int Id { get; set; }

    private bool isEditMode => Navigation.Uri.Contains("/edit");
    private StandardGradeMappingDto? gradeMapping;
    private UpdateGradeMappingRequest editGrade = new();
    private bool isLoading = true;
    private bool isSubmitting;

    // 用于解决 decimal? 到 decimal 的绑定问题
    private decimal densityValue;

    protected override async Task OnInitializedAsync()
    {
        await LoadData();
    }

    private async Task LoadData()
    {
        isLoading = true;
        StateHasChanged();

        var result = await GradeMappingService.GetByIdAsync(Id);
        if (result.Success && result.Data != null)
        {
            gradeMapping = result.Data;
            editGrade = new UpdateGradeMappingRequest
            {
                StandardGrade = gradeMapping.StandardGrade,
                PlantGrade = gradeMapping.PlantGrade,
                Density = gradeMapping.Density,
                HeatTreatment = gradeMapping.HeatTreatment,
                SpecialMaterial = gradeMapping.SpecialMaterial,
                SpecialNote = gradeMapping.SpecialNote,
                Remark = gradeMapping.Remark
            };
            // 初始化局部变量
            densityValue = gradeMapping.Density;
        }

        isLoading = false;
        StateHasChanged();
    }

    private void EnterEditMode()
    {
        Navigation.NavigateTo($"/grade-mappings/{Id}/edit");
    }

    private async Task SaveGradeMapping()
    {
        if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(editGrade.StandardGrade))
        {
            Snackbar.Add("标准牌号不能为空", Severity.Warning);
            return;
        }

        if (string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(editGrade.PlantGrade))
        {
            Snackbar.Add("工厂牌号不能为空", Severity.Warning);
            return;
        }

        // 将局部变量赋值回 editGrade
        editGrade.Density = densityValue;

        if (editGrade.Density == null || editGrade.Density <= 0)
        {
            Snackbar.Add("密度必须大于0", Severity.Warning);
            return;
        }

        isSubmitting = true;
        StateHasChanged();

        var result = await GradeMappingService.UpdateAsync(Id, editGrade);
        if (result != null && result.Success)
        {
            Snackbar.Add("更新成功", Severity.Success);
            Navigation.NavigateTo($"/grade-mappings/{Id}");
        }
        else
        {
            Snackbar.Add(result?.Message ?? "更新失败", Severity.Error);
        }

        isSubmitting = false;
        StateHasChanged();
    }

    private void GoBack()
    {
        Navigation.NavigateTo("/grade-mappings");
    }
}

@page "/grade-mappings"
@using MES.Blazor.Services
@using MES.Core.DTOs
@using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Authorization
@inject IGradeMappingService GradeMappingService
@inject NavigationManager Navigation
@inject ISnackbar Snackbar
@inject IDialogService DialogService
@attribute [Authorize(Roles = "OrderStaff,OrderDirector,Admin")]

<MudContainer MaxWidth="MaxWidth.Large" Class="mt-4">
    <MudCard>
        <MudCardHeader>
            <CardHeaderContent>
                <MudText Typo="Typo.h5" Class="font-weight-bold">
                    <MudIcon Icon="@Icons.Material.Filled.Science" Class="mr-2" Color="Color.Primary" />
                    牌号对照管理
                </MudText>
                <MudText Typo="Typo.body2" Color="Color.Secondary">标准牌号 ↔ 工厂牌号 映射配置</MudText>
            </CardHeaderContent>
            <CardHeaderActions>
                <MudButton Variant="Variant.Filled" 
                           Color="Color.Primary" 
                           StartIcon="@Icons.Material.Filled.Add"
                           OnClick="NavigateToCreate">
                    新建牌号
                </MudButton>
            </CardHeaderActions>
        </MudCardHeader>

        <MudCardContent>
            <!-- 搜索栏 -->
            <MudGrid>
                <MudItem xs="12" md="8">
                    <MudTextField T="string"
                                  Label="搜索标准牌号/工厂牌号"
                                  Immediate="true"
                                  Adornment="Adornment.End"
                                  AdornmentIcon="@Icons.Material.Filled.Search"
                                  @bind-Value="searchKeyword"
                                  @bind-Value:event="oninput"
                                  OnKeyDown="OnSearchKeyDown" />
                </MudItem>
                <MudItem xs="12" md="4">
                    <MudButton Variant="Variant.Outlined" 
                               Color="Color.Primary" 
                               FullWidth="true"
                               OnClick="Search">
                        搜索
                    </MudButton>
                </MudItem>
            </MudGrid>

            <!-- 表格 -->
            <MudTable Items="@gradeMappings" Loading="@isLoading" Dense="true" Hover="true" Class="mt-4">
                <HeaderContent>
                    <MudTh>标准牌号</MudTh>
                    <MudTh>工厂牌号</MudTh>
                    <MudTh>密度(g/cm³)</MudTh>
                    <MudTh>热处理工艺</MudTh>
                    <MudTh>特殊材料</MudTh>
                    <MudTh>操作</MudTh>
                </HeaderContent>
                <RowTemplate>
                    <MudTd>@context.StandardGrade</MudTd>
                    <MudTd>@context.PlantGrade</MudTd>
                    <MudTd>@context.Density.ToString("F4")</MudTd>
                    <MudTd>@context.HeatTreatment</MudTd>
                    <MudTd>
                        <MudChip Size="Size.Small" Color="@(context.SpecialMaterial ? Color.Warning : Color.Default)">
                            @(context.SpecialMaterial ? "特殊" : "常规")
                        </MudChip>
                    </MudTd>
                    <MudTd>
                        <MudButton Variant="Variant.Text" Size="Size.Small" Color="Color.Info" OnClick="() => ViewGradeMapping(context.Id)">查看</MudButton>
                        <MudButton Variant="Variant.Text" Size="Size.Small" Color="Color.Warning" OnClick="() => EditGradeMapping(context.Id)">编辑</MudButton>
                        <MudButton Variant="Variant.Text" Size="Size.Small" Color="Color.Error" OnClick="() => DeleteGradeMapping(context.Id)">删除</MudButton>
                    </MudTd>
                </RowTemplate>
                <PagerContent>
                    <MudTablePager />
                </PagerContent>
            </MudTable>
        </MudCardContent>
    </MudCard>
</MudContainer>

@code {
    private List<StandardGradeMappingDto> gradeMappings = new();
    private List<StandardGradeMappingDto> allGradeMappings = new();
    private bool isLoading = true;
    private string searchKeyword = string.Empty;

    protected override async Task OnInitializedAsync()
    {
        await LoadData();
    }

    private async Task LoadData()
    {
        isLoading = true;
        StateHasChanged();

        allGradeMappings = await GradeMappingService.GetAllAsync();
        ApplyFilter();

        isLoading = false;
        StateHasChanged();
    }

    private void ApplyFilter()
    {
        var query = allGradeMappings.AsEnumerable();

        if (!string.IsNullOrEmpty(searchKeyword))
        {
            query = query.Where(x => 
                x.StandardGrade.Contains(searchKeyword, StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase) ||
                x.PlantGrade.Contains(searchKeyword, StringComparison.OrdinalIgnoreCase));
        }

        gradeMappings = query.OrderBy(x => x.StandardGrade).ToList();
    }

    private void Search()
    {
        ApplyFilter();
    }

    private void OnSearchKeyDown(KeyboardEventArgs args)
    {
        if (args.Key == "Enter")
        {
            Search();
        }
    }

    private void NavigateToCreate()
    {
        Navigation.NavigateTo("/grade-mappings/create");
    }

    private void ViewGradeMapping(int id)
    {
        Navigation.NavigateTo($"/grade-mappings/{id}");
    }

    private void EditGradeMapping(int id)
    {
        Navigation.NavigateTo($"/grade-mappings/{id}/edit");
    }

    private async Task DeleteGradeMapping(int id)
    {
        bool? confirmed = await DialogService.ShowMessageBox(
            "确认删除",
            "确定要删除该牌号对照吗？\n\n如果该牌号已被订单使用，删除后可能导致数据问题！",
            yesText: "删除", cancelText: "取消");

        if (confirmed == true)
        {
            var result = await GradeMappingService.DeleteAsync(id);
            if (result != null && result.Success)
            {
                Snackbar.Add("删除成功", Severity.Success);
                await LoadData();
            }
            else
            {
                Snackbar.Add(result?.Message ?? "删除失败", Severity.Error);
            }
        }
    }
}
